***пробраться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a> (6785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">прабрацца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prabracca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">пробратися</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probratysja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probrátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробираться.html>пробира́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to make one's way, to thread one's way, to pick one's way, to edge through
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2015</b> July 28,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>Ру́сская</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жба</a> Би-би-си</cite>  | <cite>Russian BBC Service</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сообщить.html>сообщи́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вторник.html>вто́рник</a> компа́ния-опера́тор Eurotunnel, <a href = vnd.unilang:накануне.html>накану́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:около.html>о́коло</a> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяч</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелегальный.html>нелега́льных</a> мигра́нтов <a href = vnd.unilang:пытаться.html>пыта́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штурм.html>шту́рмом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:терминал.html>термина́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туннель.html>тунне́ля</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> ла-ма́ншем <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>кале́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пытаться.html>пыта́ясь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пробраться.html>пробра́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> великобрита́нию.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kak soobščíla vo vtórnik kompánija-operátor Eurotunnel, nakanúne nóčʹju ókolo 2 týsjač nelegálʹnyx migrántov pytálisʹ vzjatʹ štúrmom terminál tunnɛ́lja pod La-Mánšem v Kalé, pytájasʹ <b>probrátʹsja</b> v Velikobritániju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">As the operating company Eurotunnel reported on Tuesday, nearly 2 thousand illegal migrants tried to take the terminal of the tunnel by storm under the English Channel in Calais yesterday night, while <b>making their way</b> into Great Britain.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пробра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробудиться.html>пробуди́ться</a> (11662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробудить.html>пробуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробудиться.html>пробуди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">probudítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробуждаться.html>пробужда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to awaken, to wake up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to life <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">about nature, humanity, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробудить.html>пробуди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">probudítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***пробурчать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробурчать.html>пробурча́ть</a> (10061)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурчать.html>бурча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">burčátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пробурчать.html>пробурча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proburčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бурчать.html>бурча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grumble, to rumble <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a low growling or rumbling stomach noise</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to grumble, to complain</li>
<li>to mutter, to mumble</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a> (20124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proválivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to botch up, to ruin, to mess up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in the imperative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get lost
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливай</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>proválivaj</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">off/away with you!; make yourself scarce!; buzz off!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a> (7935)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proválivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall through, to come down</li>
<li>to fail, to flunk (on an exam)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proválivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***провалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a> (17118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:валить.html>вали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">valítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливать.html>прова́ливать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to botch up, to ruin, to mess up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin things; make a mess of things; mess things up; gum up the works</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роль.html>роль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> rolʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin ones part</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> ekzámen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fail/flunk an exam</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:письменный.html>пи́сьменном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экзамен.html>экза́мене</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> kovó-libo na písʹmennom ekzámene</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fail smb in the written paper</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оппозиция.html>оппози́ция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правительство.html>прави́тельства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oppozícija <b>provalíla</b> plan pravítelʹstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the opposition torpedoed the government's plan</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:законопроект.html>законопрое́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹ</b> zakonoproékt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kill the bill</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a> (3570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provalítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проваливаться.html>прова́ливаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fall through, to come down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потолок.html>потоло́к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">potolók <b>provalílsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the ceiling has come down</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сквозь.html>сквозь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́лся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak skvozʹ zémlju <b>provalílsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">vanished into thin air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> ...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹsja</b> mne na étom méste, jésli ...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'll be damned if ...</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fail, to flunk (on an exam)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:провалиться.html>провали́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:треск.html>тре́ском</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>provalítʹsja</b> s tréskom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn out a complete fiasco</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провалить.html>провали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***проведать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проведать.html>прове́дать</a> (13444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ведать.html>ве́дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">védatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведать.html>прове́дать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provédatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прове́дывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to see, to call <i>(on)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find out, to learn <i>(of, about)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ние</a> (3447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проводить.html>проводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">provodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provedénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проведение.html>проведе́ний</a></b>)

<li>carrying out, realization, implementation</li>

***провезти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:провезти.html>провезти́</a> (25234)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провезти.html>провезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:провозить.html>провози́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transport, to convey

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проверить.html>прове́рить</a> (1352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:верить.html>ве́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">véritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проверить.html>прове́рить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">provéritʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проверять.html>проверя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to examine, to check, to control, to verify, to test, to audit</li></ol>
